-- SELECT

-- Select All
SELECT *
FROM Sales

-- Select Columns
SELECT SalesKey, SalesAmount
FROM Sales

--Select TOP
SELECT TOP 10 *
FROM Sales

--Select 10 of the whole table
SELECT TOP 10 percent *
FROM Sales

-- Select DISTINCT y ORDER BY DESC y ASC
SELECT distinct(ProductKey)
FROM Sales
ORDER BY ProductKey DESC

-- Select WHERE & Arthmetical OPERATORS

-- [= EQUAL, > GREATER THAN, < LESS THAN, <> NOT EQUAL]

SELECT *
FROM Date
WHERE Año != 2017 -- diferente a 2017
--WHERE Año <> 2018 -- todos los años except 2018
--WHERE Año = 'diciembre'
--WHERE Fecha = '2018-01-01 00:00:00.000'

-- AND
SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE ContinentName = 'Asia'
AND RegionCountryName = 'Pakistan'

-- BETWEEN
SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE GeographyKey BETWEEN 270 AND 280

--IN
SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE ContinentName IN ('Asia', 'Europe')

--LIKE
SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE RegionCountryName LIKE '%NIA' --con terminacion en NIA

SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE RegionCountryName LIKE 'A%' -- que inician con A

SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE RegionCountryName LIKE '%ia%' -- que presentan en su nombre las letas "ia"

-- Alternative options:
-- WHERE origin_city_name LIKE '____, FL'

-- NOT
SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE ContinentName NOT IN ('Asia', 'Europe')

-- OR
SELECT *
FROM Geography
WHERE ContinentName = 'Asia'
OR RegionCountryName = 'Pakistan'

--FILTERING (using HAVING)

-- GROUP BY & HAVING
-- Alias en Columnas (renombrando)

-- Renombrar Columnas con un Alias

SELECT
ColorID ID, -- agregando ID
ColorName AS Color -- agregando AS
FROM Product
GROUP BY -- al utilizar Group By debo invocar las columnas por su nombre original
ColorID,
ColorName
HAVING
ColorID >= 10
ORDER BY
ColorID

-- Alternatively we can use HAVINGlike the following lines:
-- HAVING AVG(p.column_name > 15
-- AND AVG(p.column_name > 15;

-- Predicados
-- IS NULL

SELECT *
FROM Promotion
WHERE PromotionName IS NULL

--IS NOT NULL

SELECT *
FROM Promotion
WHERE PromotionName IS NOT NULL

--Funciones Logicas

-- IIF%

SELECT NumeroMes,
IIF(NumeroMes <= 6, 'Semestre 1', 'Semestre 2') AS Semestre
FROM Date
GROUP BY NumeroMes
ORDER BY NumeroMes

-- CASE WHEN

SELECT NumeroMes,
CASE
WHEN NumeroMes IN (1, 2, 3) THEN 'Q1'
WHEN NumeroMes IN (4, 5, 6) THEN 'Q2'
WHEN NumeroMes IN (7, 8, 9) THEN 'Q3'
WHEN NumeroMes IN (10, 11, 12) THEN 'Q4'
ELSE 'No Existe' END AS Trimestre
FROM Date
GROUP BY  NumeroMes
ORDER BY NumeroMes

-- CHOOSE

SELECT NumeroMes,
CHOOSE (NumeroMes, 'Ene', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Abr', 'May', 'Jun') AS Mes_Abrev
FROM  Date
GROUP BY NumeroMes
ORDER BY NumeroMes1

-- Funciones de Extraccion de Fechas

-- GetDate

SELECT GETDATE() AS Fecha_Actual

-- YEAR

SELECT
Fecha,
YEAR(Fecha) AS Year
FROM Date

-- MONTH

SELECT
Fecha,
MONTH(Fecha) AS Month
FROM Date

-- DAY

SELECT
Fecha,
DAY(Fecha) AS Day
FROM Date

-- DATEPART

SELECT *
Fecha,
DATEPART(QQ,Fecha) AS Trimestre
FROM Date

-- DATENAME

SELECT *
Fecha,
DATENAME(MM,Fecha) AS Mes
FROM Date

-- DATEFROMPARTS

SELECT *
Fecha,
DATEFROMPARTS(Año,NumeroMes,Dia) AS Fecha_Nueva
FROM Date

-- funciones de Fechas
-- Modificacion, Validacion e Intervalos

--DATEADD

SELECT
StartDate,
DATEADD(DD,8, StartDate) AS Fecha_Nueva
FROM Promotion

--EOMONTH

SELECT
StartDate,
EOMONTH(StartDate) AS Fin_Mes
FROM Promotion

--DATEDIFF

SELECT
StartDate,
EndDate,
DATEDIFF(DD,StartDate, EndDate) AS Diferencia_Fechas
FROM Promotion

--ISDATE

SELECT
StartDate,
ISDATE(StartDate) AS Fecha -- Esto me devuelve un Booleano como resultado de la evaluacion (1=True, 0=False)
FROM Promotion


-- Funciones de Texto Basicas

-- CONCAT

SELECT
BrandName,
ColorName,
CONCAT(BrandName, '-', ColorName) AS Marca_Color
FROM Product

-- CONCAT_WS (Esta sentencia es mas rapida y recomendable que la anterior (CONCAT)

SELECT
BrandName,
ColorName,
CONCAT_WS('-', BrandName, ColorName, ProductLabel) AS Concatenar
FROM Product

-- LEFT

SELECT
ColorName,
LEFT(ColorName, 3) AS Inic_Color
FROM Product

-- RIGHT

SELECT
ColorName,
RIGHT(ColorName, 3) AS Inic_Color
FROM Product

-- LOWER

SELECT
ColorName,
LOWER(ColorName) AS Miniscula
FROM Product

-- UPPER

SELECT
ColorName,
UPPER(ColorName) AS Mayuscula
FROM Product

-- REPLACE

SELECT
ProductName,
REPLACE(ProductName, 'Contoso', 'GrowUp') AS Nombres_Producto
FROM Product

-- SPACE

SELECT
ProductName,
CONCAT(SPACE(5), ProductName) AS Columna_Producto
FROM Product

-- LTRIM

SELECT
ProductName,
LTRIM(CONCAT(SPACE(5), ProductName)) AS Columna_Producto_Correcta,
CONCAT(SPACE(5), ProductName) AS Columna_Producto_Mal
FROM Product

-- RTRIM

SELECT
ProductName,
RTRIM(CONCAT(ProductName, SPACE(5))) AS Columna_Producto_Correcta,
CONCAT(ProductName, SPACE(5)) AS Columna_Producto_Mal
FROM Product

--TRIM

SELECT
ProductName,
TRIM(CONCAT(SPACE(5),ProductName,SPACE(5))) AS Columna_Producto_Correcta,
CONCAT(ProductName, SPACE(5)) AS Columna_Producto_Mal
FROM

-- Funciones de Texto Avanzadas

-- LEN (Extrae el largo de una columna)

SELECT
StoreName,
LEN(StoreName) AS Largo
FROM Stores

-- CHARINDEX (Me indica la posicion de un Index)

-- En estos dos casos sgtes va a buscar la posicion del campo vacio

SELECT
StoreName,
CHARINDEX(' ',StoreName) AS Posicion
FROM Stores

SELECT
StoreName,
CHARINDEX(' ',StoreName,9) AS Posicion
FROM Stores

-- SUBSTRING (Nos permite utilizar la funcion LEN y CHARINDEX juntos)

SELECT
StoreName,
SUBSTRING(StoreName,CHARINDEX(' ',StoreName),LEN(StoreName)) AS Ciudad
FROM Stores

-- Funciones de Conversion

-- CAST

SELECT
DiscountAmount,
CAST(DiscountAmount as int) Descuento -- No puedo utilizar "AS Descuento" ya que fue utilizado dentro del bracket.
FROM Sales

-- CONVERT

SELECT
DiscountAmount,
SalesQuantity,
CONVERT(decimal(10,2),SalesQuantity) as Cantidad
FROM Sales

-- TRY CAST
SELECT
CASE WHEN TRY_CAST('GrowUp' as float) is null --CASE WHEN para hacer una funcion logica
THEN 'Fallido'
ELSE 'Exitoso'
END AS Resultado

-- TRY CONVERT

SELECT
CASE WHEN TRY_CONVERT(float, 'GrowUp') is null --CASE WHEN para hacer una funcion logica
THEN 'Fallido'
ELSE 'Exitoso'
END AS Resultado

-- ROUND

SELECT
DiscountAmount,
ROUND(DiscountAmount,1) AS Redondeo
FROM Sales

-- Funciones para Nulos

-- COALESCE
-- Este primer paso es para consultar un registro con un campo tipo null
Select *
FROM Registro_Nacional
WHERE Cedula = 115400138

--Aplicar el COALESCE
Select
Nombre,
Primer_Apellido,
Segundo_Apellido,
COALESCE(Segundo_Apellido, 'Solis') AS Seg_Apellido
FROM Registro_Nacional
WHERE Cedula = 115400138

-- IS NULL

Select
Nombre,
Primer_Apellido,
Segundo_Apellido,
ISNULL(Segundo_Apellido, 'SOLIS') AS Seg_Apellido
FROM Registro_Nacional
WHERE Cedula = 115400138


-- SQL JOIN

-- JOIN

-- Consultamos la tabla Store

SELECT *
FROM Geography

-- INNER JOIN [alternatively you can indicate the word: JOIN instead of INNERJOIN]

SELECT
Stores.Geography_Key,
Geography.ContinentName
FROM Stores INNER JOIN Geography
ON Stores.Geography_Key = Geography.GeographyKey


-- INNER JOIN RENOMBRANDO LAS TABLAS

SELECT
A.Geography_Key,
B.ContinentName
FROM Stores A INNER JOIN Geography B
ON A.Geography_Key = B.GeographyKey

-- LEFT JOIN

SELECT
A.SalesKey,
A.SalesAmount,
B.StoreDescription
FROM Sales A LEFT JOIN Stores B
ON A.StoreKey = B.Store_Key

-- RIGHT JOIN

SELECT
A.Store_Key,
B.SalesAmount
FROM Stores A RIGHT JOIN Sales B
ON A.Store_Key = B.StoreKey

-- OUTER JOINS (Right Join & Left Join)

-- LEFT OUTER JOIN
-- (Todos los campos de la Tabla A que no estan presentes en la Tabla B)
-- Este tipo de consulta nos permite identificar aquellos que estan en la tabla B que estan vacios y que deberian ser corregidos

SELECT *
FROM Date

SELECT*
FROM Date A LEFT OUTER JOIN Sales B
ON A.Fecha = B.DateKey
WHERE B.DateKey IS NULL

-- RIGHT OUTER JOIN
-- Esta consulta nos permite al igual que el caso anterior identificar aquellos registros de la Tabla A que deben ser corregidos debido a q se encuentran vacios.

SELECT *
FROM Sales A RIGHT OUTER JOIN Date B
ON A.DateKey = B.Fecha
WHERE A.DateKey IS NULL

-- FULL JOIN & FULL OUTER JOIN
--1. Todos los datos
--2. Datos que no se encuentran relacionados de las 2 tablas

SELECT *
FROM Date

SELECT*
FROM Sales A FULL JOIN Date B
ON A.DateKey = B.Fecha

SELECT*
FROM Sales A FULL OUTER JOIN Date B
ON A.DateKey = B.Fecha
WHERE A.DateKey IS NULL
OR B.Fecha IS NULL


--Operaciones Matematicas Basicas

-- RESTA entre Columnas

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
A.TotalCost,
A.SalesAmount,
A.SalesAmount - A.TotalCost AS Variacion
FROM Sales A INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey = B.Channel_Key

-- SUMA entre Columnas

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
A.TotalCost,
A.SalesAmount,
A.SalesAmount + A.TotalCost AS SumAmount
FROM Sales A INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey = B.Channel_Key

-- DIVISION entre Columnas

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
A.TotalCost,
A.SalesAmount,
ROUND((A.SalesAmount - A.TotalCost) / A.SalesAmount,2) AS Porcentaje_Variacion
FROM Sales A INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey = B.Channel_Key

-- MULTIPLICACION entre Columnas

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
A.TotalCost,
A.SalesAmount,
A.SalesAmount * A.TotalCost AS Total
FROM Sales A INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey = B.Channel_Key


-- Funciones de Agregacion

-- SUM
-- OJO: siempre que utilice una funcion de agregacion debera de utilizar un Group By al final del Query

Select
ProductKey,
SUM(SalesAmount) AS Venta
FROM Sales
GROUP BY
ProductKey

Select *
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key

Select *
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha

Select *
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019

Select
B.ChannelName,
UPPER(LEFT(Mes,3)) AS Mes,
SUM(SalesAmount) as Venta
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
C.Mes,
NumeroMes
HAVING
SUM(SalesAmount) > 20000000
ORDER BY
ChannelName,
NumeroMes DESC

-- AVG TOTAL Y AVG DISTINTIVA

Select
B.ChannelName,
UPPER(LEFT(Mes,3)) AS Mes,
AVG(SalesAmount) as Media,
AVG(DISTINCT(SalesAmount)) as Media_Dist
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
C.Mes,
NumeroMes
ORDER BY
ChannelName,
NumeroMes DESC

-- AGGREGATE FUNCTIONS (COUNT, SUM, AVG, MIN, MAX)

-- COUNT - DISTINCT COUNT

Select
B.ChannelName,
UPPER(LEFT(Mes,3)) AS Mes,
COUNT(SalesAmount) as Conteo,
COUNT(DISTINCT(SalesAmount)) as Conteo_Disnt
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
C.Mes,
NumeroMes
ORDER BY
ChannelName,
NumeroMes DESC

-- MAX

Select
B.ChannelName,
UPPER(LEFT(Mes,3)) AS Mes,
MAX(SalesAmount) as Venta_Max
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
C.Mes,
NumeroMes
ORDER BY
ChannelName,
NumeroMes DESC


-- MIN

Select
B.ChannelName,
UPPER(LEFT(Mes,3)) AS Mes,
MIN(SalesAmount) as Venta_Max
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
C.Mes,
NumeroMes
ORDER BY
ChannelName,
NumeroMes DESC

-- VAR

Select
B.ChannelName,
UPPER(LEFT(Mes,3)) AS Mes,
VAR(SalesAmount) as Varianza,
VAR(DISTINCT(SalesAmount)) as Varianza_dist
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
C.Mes,
NumeroMes
ORDER BY
ChannelName,
NumeroMes DESC

-- DEST ESTANDARD

Select
B.ChannelName,
UPPER(LEFT(Mes,3)) AS Mes,
STDEV(SalesAmount) as Desviacion,
STDEV(DISTINCT(SalesAmount)) as Desviacion_Disnt
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	 = B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
C.Mes,
NumeroMes
ORDER BY
ChannelName,
NumeroMes DESC

-- Funciones Matematicas

-- ABS (Valor Absoluto)

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
A.SalesAmount,
ABS(SalesAmount) AS Valor_Abs
FROM Sales A INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.ChannelKey = B.Channel_Key

-- POWER (Potencia)

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
A.SalesAmount,
POWER(A.SalesAmount,2) AS Potencia
FROM Sales A INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.ChannelKey = B.Channel_Key

-- SQRT (Raiz Cuadrada)

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
A.SalesAmount,
SQRT(SalesAmount) AS Raiz
FROM Sales A INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.ChannelKey = B.Channel_Key

-- Comando UNION

SELECT
B.ChannelName,
E.RegionCountryName,
C.Mes,
C.Año,
SUM(A.SalesAmount) AS Venta
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	= B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
LEFT JOIN Stores D
ON A.StoreKey = D.Store_Key
INNER JOIN Geography E
ON D.Geography_Key = E.GeographyKey
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
E.RegionCountryName,
C.Mes,
C.Año

(SELECT
B.ChannelName,
E.RegionCountryName,
C.Mes,
C.Año,
SUM(A.SalesAmount) AS Venta
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	= B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
LEFT JOIN Stores D
ON A.StoreKey = D.Store_Key
INNER JOIN Geography E
ON D.Geography_Key = E.GeographyKey
WHERE C.Año = 2019
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
E.RegionCountryName,
C.Mes,
C.Año
UNION
SELECT
B.ChannelName,
E.RegionCountryName,
C.Mes,
C.Año,
SUM(A.SalesAmount) AS Venta
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.channelKey	= B.Channel_Key
INNER JOIN Date C
ON A.DateKey = C.Fecha
LEFT JOIN Stores D
ON A.StoreKey = D.Store_Key
INNER JOIN Geography E
ON D.Geography_Key = E.GeographyKey
WHERE C.Año = 2018
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
E.RegionCountryName,
C.Mes,
C.Año)


-- Estructuras Complejas

-- Select Anidados o Subconsultas

-- Analisis de la Vta de Productos del 1 a 100 en Tiendas de Asia y Europa,
-- cuando la cantidad de empleados por tienda sea superior a 10
-- y la Marca sea la Aceptada y el resto denegada

SELECT *
FROM Sales

SELECT
A.ProductKey,
B.ChannelName,
IIF(A.ProductKey IN ((SELECT Product_key FROM Product WHERE BrandName = 'Contoso')),'Aceptado','+Denegado') as Tipo,
SUM(A.SalesAmount) as Venta,
SUM(A.totalCost) as Costo,
SUM(A.SalesAmount) - SUM(A.TotalCost) AS Variacion
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.ChannelKey = B. channel_Key
WHERE A.StoreKey IN
(
SELECT
A.Store_Key
FROM Stores A
INNER JOIN Geography B
ON A.Geography_Key = B.GeographyKey
WHERE B.ContinentName LIKE 'ASIA'
OR B.ContinentName LIKE 'EUROPA'
AND A.EmployeeCount > 10
)
AND A.ProductKey BETWEEN 1 AND 100
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
A.ProductKey

-- Creacion de Vistas
-- Esto es una Tabla Virtual que se accesa mediante una consulta

CREATE VIEW VentasGerencia AS

SELECT
A.ProductKey,
B.ChannelName,
IIF(A.ProductKey IN ((SELECT Product_key FROM Product WHERE BrandName = 'Contoso')),'Aceptado','+Denegado') as Tipo,
SUM(A.SalesAmount) as Venta,
SUM(A.totalCost) as Costo,
SUM(A.SalesAmount) - SUM(A.TotalCost) AS Variacion
FROM Sales A
INNER JOIN Channel B
ON A.ChannelKey = B. channel_Key
WHERE A.StoreKey IN
(
SELECT
A.Store_Key
FROM Stores A
INNER JOIN Geography B
ON A.Geography_Key = B.GeographyKey
WHERE B.ContinentName LIKE 'ASIA'
OR B.ContinentName LIKE 'EUROPA'
AND A.EmployeeCount > 10
)
AND A.ProductKey BETWEEN 1 AND 100
GROUP BY
B.ChannelName,
A.ProductKey

--CREATE TABLE
--Syntaxis:
CREATE TABLE table_name(
column_name TYPE column_constraint,
column_name TYPE column_constraint,
table_contraint table_contraint
)INHERITS existing_table_name;

CREATE TABLE account(
user_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
user_name VARCHAR (50)UNIQUE NOT NULL,
password VARCHAR (50) NOT NULL,
email VARCHAR (250) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
created_on TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
last_login TIMESTAMP --el constraint no es mandatory
)

CREATE TABLE job(
job_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
job_name VARCHAR (200)UNIQUE NOT NULL
)

CREATE TABLE account_job(
user_id INTEGER REFERENCES account(user_id), --FK
job_id INTEGER REFERENCES job(job_id),
hire_date TIMESTAMP
)

--INSERT TABLE
--Syntaxis:
INSERT INTO table(col1, col2,...)
SELECT col1, col2,...
FROM another_table
WHERE condition;

INSERT INTO account(user_name,password,email,created_on)
VALUES
('Jose','password','jose@mail.com',CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)

INSERT INTO job(job_name)
VALUES
('Astronaut'),
('President')

INSERT INTO account_job(user_id, job_id, hire_date)
VALUES
(1, 1, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)

--INSERT TABLE
--Syntaxis:
UPDATE table
SET col1 = value1,
	col2 = value2, ...
WHERE
	condition;

UPDATE account
SET last_login = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP

SELECT * FROM account --verifiquemos los cambios aplicados

UPDATE account
SET last_login = created_on

SELECT * FROM account

UPDATE account_job
SET hire_date = account.created_on
FROM account
WHERE account_job.user_id = account.user_id

SELECT * FROM account

UPDATE account
SET last_login = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
RETURNING email, created_on, last_login

--DELETE TABLE
--Syntaxis:
DELETE FROM table
WHERE row_id = 1

INSERT INTO job(job_name)
VALUES ('Cowboy')

SELECT *
FROM job

DELETE FROM job
WHERE job_name = 'Cowboy'
RETURNING job_id,job_name

--ALTER TABLE
--Syntaxis:
--Adding Columns:
ALTER TABLE table_name
ADD COLUMN new_col TYPE
--Removing Columns:
ALTER TABLE table_name
DROP COLUMN col_name
--Alter Contrains:
ALTER TABLE table_name
ALTER COLUMN col_name
SET DEFAULT value --(*)
--(*) or
SET NOT NULL
--(*) or
ADD CONSTRAINT constraint_name

CREATE TABLE information(
info_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
person VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL UNIQUE
)

ALTER TABLE information
RENAME TO new_info

SELECT *
FROM new_info

ALTER TABLE new_info
RENAME COLUMN person TO people

SELECT *
FROM new_info

--DROP TABLE
--Syntaxis:
--Remove all Dependencies
ALTER TABLE table_name
DROP COLUMN col_name CASCADE
--Check for existence to avoid error
ALTER TABLE table_name
DROP COLUMN IF EXISTS col_name
--Drop Multiple Tables
ALTER TABLE table_name
DROP COLUMN col_one
DROP COLUMN col_two

ALTER TABLE new_info
DROP COLUMN person

SELECT  *
FROM new_info

ALTER TABLE new_info
DROP COLUMN IF EXISTS person

--CHECK CONSTRAINT
--Syntaxis:
CREATE TABLE example(
num_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
age SMALLINT CHECK (age > 21),
parent_age SMALLINT CHECK(parent_age > age)
);

CREATE TABLE employees(
emp_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
first_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
last_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
birthday DATE CHECK (birthday > '1900-01-01'),
hire_date DATE CHECK (hire_date > birthday),
salary INTEGER CHECK (salary > 0)
)

INSERT INTO employees(
first_name,
last_name,
birthday,
hire_date,
salary
)
VALUES
('Sammy', 'Smith', '1990-10-03', '2009-01-01', 100)

SELECT *
FROM employees

--ASSESTMENT TEST 3
CREATE TABLE teachers(
	teacher_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
	first_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	last_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	homeroom_number INTEGER,
	department VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	email VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
	phone VARCHAR(20) UNIQUE
);

CREATE TABLE students(
	student_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
	first_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	last_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	homeroom_number INTEGER,
	phone VARCHAR(20) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
	email VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE,
	graduation_year INTEGER
);

INSERT INTO students(student_id, first_name, last_name, homeroom_number,
					phone, graduation_year)
VALUES ('1','Mark','Watney','5','7775551234','2035');

INSERT INTO teachers(teacher_id, first_name, last_name, homeroom_number,
					department, email, phone)
VALUES ('1','Jonas','Salk','5','Biology','jsalk@school.org','7775554321')

SELECT *
FROM students
SELECT *
FROM teachers


-- TRABAJO ILUSTRATIVO

-- Creacion de tablas
	CREATE TABLE Provincias(
		ID_Provincia varchar(5) not null,
		Nombre varchar(20) not null,
		PRIMARY KEY (ID_Provincia)
		);
	CREATE TABLE Materias(
		ID_Materia varchar(10) not null,
		Nombre varchar(50) not null,
		ID_Profesor varchar(30) not null,
		PRIMARY KEY (ID_Materia)
		);
	CREATE TABLE Calificaciones(
		ID_Estudiante varchar(10) not null,
		ID_Materia varchar(10) not null,
		Nota varchar(2) not null
		);
	CREATE TABLE Personas(
		ID varchar(10) not null,
		Nombre varchar(20) not null,
		Apellido varchar(20) not null,
		Genero char(1) not null,
		ID_Provincia varchar(10) not null,
		PRIMARY KEY (ID)
		);

		-- Creacion de llaves primarias

	Alter table Provincias
	   add primary key (ID_Provincia)
	Alter table Materias
	   add primary key (ID_Materia)};
	Alter table Calificaciones

	-- Querys

	--***Query_A:***
	--Nombre de Provincia,
	--Nombre del estudiante,
	--Apellido del estudiante,
	--Nombre de materia,
	--Notas, y
	--ordenado de forma descendente por el nombre de la provincia.

SELECT p.nombre, pe.nombre, apellido, m.nombre, nota --los 5 campos q se solicitan explicitamente para trabajar
FROM provincias AS p -- 1ra tabla en terminos de Abreviatura
INNER JOIN personas AS pe -- 2da tabla Abrev.
ON  p.id_provincia = pe.id_provincia --aca se deben estipular los campos llave (analogos) q existen entre la tabla A y la tabla B. Estructurado: Table_name+Field_name
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON pe.id = c.id_estudiante
INNER JOIN materias AS m
ON m.id_materias = c.id_materia
ORDER BY p.nombre DESC

	--***Query_B:***
	--Nombre del Profesor,
	--Nombre de materia,
	--Cantidad de Estudiantes,
	--Promedio de Notas.

SELECT id_profesor, m.nombre, p.nombre,
COUNT(p.nombre) AS cn
--AVG(nota) comentario: tengo duda que no me funcione, debe ser x el type de la Columna
FROM materias AS m
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON  m.id_materias = c.id_materia
INNER JOIN personas AS p
ON p.id = c.id_estudiante
GROUP BY id_profesor, m.nombre, p.nombre
ORDER BY cn

	--***Query_C:***
	--Provincia,
	--Materia,
	--Mejor Nota.

SELECT pr.id_provincia, m.nombre--, MAX(c.nota)
FROM provincias AS pr
INNER JOIN personas AS pe
ON pr.id_provincia = pe.id_provincia
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON pe.id = c.id_estudiante
INNER JOIN materias AS m
ON m.id_materias = c.id_materia
--GROUP BY c.nota

		--***Query_D:***
	--Provincia,
	--Nombre del Profesor,
	--Nombre de materia,
	--Mejor Nota,
	--Nombre del Estudiante

SELECT pr.nombre, m.id_profesor, m.nombre, MAX(nota), pe.nombre
FROM provincias AS pr
INNER JOIN personas AS pe
ON  pr.id_provincia = pe.id_provincia
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON pe.id = c.id_estudiante
INNER JOIN materias AS m
ON m.id_materias = c.id_materia
GROUP BY pr.nombre, m.id_profesor, m.nombre,pe.nombre


		--***Query_E:***
	--Provincia,
	--Nombre del Profesor,
	--Materias,
	--Promedio de Notas.

SELECT pr.nombre, m.id_profesor, m.nombre, ROUND(AVG(CAST(nota as int)))
FROM provincias AS pr
INNER JOIN personas AS pe
ON pr.id_provincia = pe.id_provincia
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON pe.id = c.id_estudiante
INNER JOIN materias AS m
ON m.id_materias = c.id_materia
GROUP BY pr.nombre, m.id_profesor, m.nombre


	--***Query_F:***
	--Promedio de notas,
	--según género,
	--para la provincia de San José,
	--y de la materia 2,

SELECT pr.nombre, pe.genero, m.nombre, ROUND(AVG(CAST(nota as int)))
FROM provincias AS pr
INNER JOIN personas AS pe
ON  pr.id_provincia = pe.id_provincia
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON pe.id = c.id_estudiante
INNER JOIN materias AS m
ON m.id_materias = c.id_materia
WHERE pr.nombre = 'San Jose' AND m.nombre = 'Quantum Intelligence'
GROUP BY pr.nombre, pe.genero, m.nombre

		--***Query_G:***
	--Estudiantes con notas mejores al promedio de cada materia.

SELECT pe.nombre, pe.id,  m.nombre, MAX(c.nota)
FROM personas AS pe
INNER JOIN provincias AS pr
ON  pr.id_provincia = pe.id_provincia
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON pe.id = c.id_estudiante
INNER JOIN materias AS m
ON m.id_materias = c.id_materia
GROUP BY pe.nombre, pe.id, m.nombre

		--***Query_H:***
	--Indicar si el estudiante aprueba la materia, colocando, si la nota es menor a 60

SELECT pe.nombre, pe.apellido, pe.id, m.nombre, ROUND(AVG(CAST(nota as int)))
FROM personas AS pe
INNER JOIN provincias AS pr
ON  pr.id_provincia = pe.id_provincia
INNER JOIN calificaciones AS c
ON pe.id = c.id_estudiante
INNER JOIN materias AS m
ON m.id_materias = c.id_materia
GROUP BY pe.nombre, pe.id, m.nombre
WHERE nota BETWEEN 1 AND 60

use testlead

-- Creacion de esquema
create schema cd02


-- Creacion de tablas
	CREATE TABLE cd02.departamento(
		pk_departamento smallint identity(1,1)  not null,
		departamento varchar(100) not null,
		habilitado bit not null
		)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.usuario(
		pk_usuario int identity(1,1)  not null,
		codigo varchar(30) not null,
		nombre varchar(50) not null,
		apellido1 varchar(50) not null,
		apellido2 varchar(50) not null,
		genero char(1) not null,
		fecha_nacimiento date null,
		edad tinyint null,
		habilitado bit not null
		)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.usuario_departamento(
		fk_usuario int not null,
		fk_departamento smallint,
		fecha_ingreso date not null
	)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.usuario_n1(
		fk_usuario_n1 int not null,
		nivel varchar(30) null
		)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.usuario_supervisor(
		fk_usuario_supervisor int not null,
		nivel varchar(30) null
		)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.grupo(
		pk_grupo smallint identity(1,1) not null,
		grupo varchar(50) not null,
		nombre varchar(100) null
	)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.grupo_supervisor(
			fk_grupo smallint not null,
			fk_usuario_supervisor int not null,
			fecha_ingreso date not null,
			fecha_finalizacion date null
		)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.grupo_usuario_n1(
			fk_grupo smallint not null,
			fk_usuario_n1 int not null,
			fecha_ingreso date not null,
			fecha_finalizacion date null
		)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.evento (
		pk_evento smallint identity(1,1) not null,
		evento varchar(50) not null,
		descripcion varchar(100) null,
		peso int
	)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.evento_usuario (
		fk_evento smallint not null,
		fk_usuario int not null,
		fk_cliente  int not null,
		fecha datetime not null,
		duracion int not null
	)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.ubicacion(
		pk_ubicacion smallint identity(1,1)  not null,
		distrito_id int not null,
		provincia varchar(50) not null,
		canton varchar(50) not null,
		distrito varchar(50) not null
	)

	CREATE TABLE cd02.cliente(
		pk_cliente int identity(1,1)  not null,
		cedula varchar(10) not null,
		nombre varchar(50) not null,
		apellido1 varchar(50) not null,
		apellido2 varchar(50) not null,
		genero char(1) not null,
		vencimiento date not null,
		fk_ubicacion smallint not null
	)

	-- Creacion de llaves primarias

	ALTER TABLE cd02.departamento
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_departamento PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (pk_departamento)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.usuario
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_usuario PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (pk_usuario)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.evento
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_evento PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (pk_evento)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.usuario_supervisor
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_usuario_supervisor PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (fk_usuario_supervisor)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.usuario_n1
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_usuario_n1 PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (fk_usuario_n1)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.grupo
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_grupo PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (pk_grupo)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.grupo_supervisor
		ADD CONSTRAINT pk_grupo_supervisor PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (fk_grupo,fk_usuario_supervisor)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.grupo_usuario_n1
		ADD CONSTRAINT pk_grupo_usuario_n1 PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (fk_grupo,fk_usuario_n1)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.ubicacion
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_ubicacion PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (pk_ubicacion)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.cliente
	   ADD CONSTRAINT pk_cliente PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED (pk_cliente)


	-- Relacion usuario-departamento
	ALTER TABLE cd02.usuario_departamento
	   ADD CONSTRAINT fk_usuario FOREIGN KEY (fk_usuario)
			REFERENCES cd02.usuario (pk_usuario)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.usuario_departamento
	   ADD CONSTRAINT fk_departamento FOREIGN KEY (fk_departamento)
			REFERENCES cd02.departamento (pk_departamento)

	-- Relacion especializacion
	ALTER TABLE cd02.usuario_n1
		ADD CONSTRAINT fk_usuario_n1 FOREIGN KEY (fk_usuario_n1)
		REFERENCES cd02.usuario (pk_usuario)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.usuario_supervisor
		ADD CONSTRAINT fk_usuario_supervisor FOREIGN KEY (fk_usuario_supervisor)
		REFERENCES cd02.usuario (pk_usuario)


	-- Relacion evento-usuario

	ALTER TABLE cd02.evento_usuario
		ADD CONSTRAINT fk_evento_usuario_evento FOREIGN KEY (fk_evento)
		REFERENCES cd02.evento (pk_evento)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.evento_usuario
		ADD CONSTRAINT fk_evento_usuario_usuario_evento FOREIGN KEY (fk_usuario)
		REFERENCES cd02.usuario (pk_usuario)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.evento_usuario
		ADD CONSTRAINT fk_cliente_evento FOREIGN KEY (fk_cliente)
		REFERENCES cd02.cliente (pk_cliente)

	-- Relacion grupo-supervisor
	ALTER TABLE cd02.grupo_supervisor
			ADD CONSTRAINT pk_fk_grupo_supervisor FOREIGN KEY (fk_grupo)
				REFERENCES cd02.grupo (pk_grupo)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.grupo_supervisor
			ADD CONSTRAINT pk_fk_usuario_supervisor FOREIGN KEY (fk_usuario_supervisor)
				REFERENCES cd02.usuario_supervisor (fk_usuario_supervisor)


	-- Relacion grupo-usuario-N1
	ALTER TABLE cd02.grupo_usuario_n1
			ADD CONSTRAINT pk_fk_grupo_usuario FOREIGN KEY (fk_grupo)
				REFERENCES cd02.grupo (pk_grupo)

	ALTER TABLE cd02.grupo_usuario_n1
			ADD CONSTRAINT pk_fk_usuario_usuario FOREIGN KEY (fk_usuario_n1)
				REFERENCES cd02.usuario_n1 (fk_usuario_n1)


	--- Relacion cliente-ubicacion
	ALTER TABLE cd02.cliente
	   ADD CONSTRAINT fk_ubicacion_cliente FOREIGN KEY (fk_ubicacion)
			REFERENCES cd02.ubicacion (pk_ubicacion)

	--- Creacion de indices
	CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX idx_cedula ON cd02.cliente( cedula ASC)

--- Eliminacion de estructuras
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.grupo
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.grupo_supervisor
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.grupo_usuario_n1

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.departamento
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.usuario
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.usuario_departamento
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.usuario_n1
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.usuario_supervisor
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.evento
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.evento_usuario
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.cliente
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS cd02.ubicacion

										provincia			 varchar(75) not null,
										canton				 varchar(75) not null,
										distrito			 varchar(75) not null)

drop table if exists datosbase.personas

									genero				 char(1) not null,
									nombre				 varchar(75) not null,
									apellido1			 varchar(75) not null,
									apellido2			 varchar(75) not null,
									ubicacionid			 int not null)

drop table if exists datosbase.productos

									producto			 varchar(250) not null,
									precio				 decimal(18,2) not null,
									categoria			 varchar(30) not null,
									descripcioncategoria varchar(250) not null)

drop table if exists datosbase.ordenes

									fecha			 datetime not null,
									clienteid		 int not null,
									empleadoid		 int not null,
									productoid		 int not null,
									preciounitario	 decimal(18,2) not null,
									cantidad		 smallint not null,
									descuento		 decimal(18,2) not null )

	-- 1.Resumen de ordenes por cantidad de órdenes generadas
--a.Cantidad de órdenes generadas

SELECT COUNT (DISTINCT [ordenid]) as CANT_ORDENES
FROM [datosbase].[ordenes]

--b. Monto promedio por orden

	SELECT SUM (preciounitario*cantidad)/ COUNT (ordenid) AS Promedioxorden
from [datosbase].[ordenes]


-- c.Cantidad de órdenes por origen
SELECT ORIGEN, COUNT(ordenid) as CONTEO
FROM (
SELECT DISTINCT
	ordenid,
	CASE
		WHEN RAND(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) > 0.5 THEN 'SITIO'
		ELSE 'WEB' END AS ORIGEN
FROM datosbase.ordenes
GROUP BY ORDENID) AS T
GROUP BY ORIGEN

--2.Resumen de ventas por categoría
--a.Monto total vendido

SELECT sum(cantidad*preciounitario) AS Montototxcateg, [categoria]
FROM [datosbase].[ordenes] LEFT JOIN [datosbase].[productos] ON [datosbase].[ordenes].productoid = [datosbase].[productos].productoid
GROUP BY categoria

--Prueba generar tabla con monto total y categoría
WITH T2 AS
	(SELECT SUM(cantidad*preciounitario) as mtototal, 'misc' as categoria
	from [datosbase].[ordenes])


SELECT  *
from datosbase.productos FULL JOIN T2 on productos.categoria = T2.categoria

--b.Cantidad de articulos vendidos
SELECT COUNT(cantidad) AS Montototxcateg, [categoria]
FROM [datosbase].[ordenes] LEFT JOIN [datosbase].[productos] ON [datosbase].[ordenes].productoid = [datosbase].[productos].productoid
GROUP BY categoria


--c.Proporción de ventas respecto al monto total de ventas
WITH TABLA AS
(
SELECT SUM(cantidad*preciounitario) AS mtoxcategoria ,[categoria], 	(SELECT SUM(cantidad*preciounitario) as mtototal
	from [datosbase].[ordenes]) as total
FROM [datosbase].[ordenes] A Left JOIN [datosbase].[productos] B ON A.productoid = B.productoid
GROUP BY categoria
)
SELECT mtoxcategoria/total as proporcion, categoria
FROM TABLA


--3. Top 5 de artículos más vendidos por supermercado (en términos de cantidad de unidades) el cual debe incluir:

--a. Cantidad vendida en sitio y web
ALTER TABLE [datosbase].[ordenes] ADD Canales sql_variant

-- Dar contenido a columna canales
	update datosbase.ordenes
	 set Canales = CASE
	 WHEN 1.0 + floor(2 * RAND(convert(varbinary, newid()))) = 1 THEN 'WEB' else 'SITIO' end
	where ordenid = (Select distinct [ordenid])--ordenid (Select distinct [ordenid])



select top 5
	cantidad,
	sitio,
	web
FROM TABLAX
ORDER BY CANTIDAD DESC

--4. Ventas totales por mes por supermercado, considerando
ALTER TABLE [datosbase].[ordenes] ADD Supermercados sql_variant

-- Dar contenido a tabla Supermercados
	update datosbase.ordenes
	 set Supermercados = CASE
	 WHEN 1.0 + floor(2 * RAND(convert(varbinary, newid()))) = 1 THEN 'Supermercado Alajuela' else 'Supermercado San José' end
	where ordenid = (Select [ordenid] )



	select *
From [datosbase].[ordenes]
